## Diagram 1

```mermaid
flowchart TD
    Start([Start Deployment]) --> CheckFVHome{FV_HOME set?}
    CheckFVHome -->|No| ExitFVHome[Exit: FV_HOME not set]
    CheckFVHome -->|Yes| CDHome[cd $FV_HOME]
    CDHome --> UpdateCode[Update code repository<br/>git pull origin $BRANCH]
    UpdateCode --> CDConfig[cd research/orchestrator/configuration]
    CDConfig --> UpdateCron[Update crontab]
    UpdateCron --> CronCheck{Crontab<br/>updated?}
    CronCheck -->|No| ExitCron[Exit: Failed to update crontab]
    CronCheck -->|Yes| CheckEnvFile{orchestrator_env311<br/>exists?}
    CheckEnvFile -->|No| ExitEnv[Exit: Environment file not found]
    CheckEnvFile -->|Yes| CheckProjectRoot{PROJECT_ROOT<br/>set?}
    CheckProjectRoot -->|Yes| CheckEnvPR{env311 dir<br/>exists in PROJECT_ROOT?}
    CheckProjectRoot -->|No| CheckEnvDefault{env311 dir<br/>exists in default path?}
    CheckEnvPR -->|Yes| InstallReqPR[pip install requirements<br/>from PROJECT_ROOT]
    CheckEnvPR -->|No| ZipGraphReduce
    CheckEnvDefault -->|Yes| InstallReqDefault[pip install requirements<br/>from default path]
    CheckEnvDefault -->|No| ZipGraphReduce
    InstallReqPR --> ZipGraphReduce
    InstallReqDefault --> ZipGraphReduce
    ZipGraphReduce{PROJECT_ROOT set<br/>and graphreduce exists?}
    ZipGraphReduce -->|Yes| ZipGR[zip graphreduce project]
    ZipGraphReduce -->|No| ZipShapely
    ZipGR --> ZipShapely{PROJECT_ROOT set<br/>and shapely exists?}
    ZipShapely -->|Yes| ZipSH[zip shapely project]
    ZipShapely -->|No| UpdateService
    ZipSH --> UpdateService[Copy luigi311.service to systemd]
    UpdateService --> Reload[systemctl daemon-reload]
    Reload --> Stop[systemctl stop luigi311.service]
    Stop --> StartSvc[systemctl start luigi311.service]
    StartSvc --> Status[systemctl status luigi311.service]
    Status --> Chown[chown -R ec2-user:ec2-user]
    Chown --> End([End])
```
